<Text>What can I say? This is, hands down, the best Italian food and pizza in San Diego! As one who grew up in northern New Jersey, I am very picky about my Italian food and pizza. This place reminds me of back home and it starts with the aroma the moment you step in the door. Tucked in the corner of a tiny La Mesa strip mall, you could be forgiven for not noticing it. However, once you go, you‚Äôre hooked. There‚Äôs simply no place like it in the area and, believe me, I‚Äôve searched in the past few decades I‚Äôve lived in San Diego. The owner, Pietro, is present almost every night and runs a great staff who make you feel at home. His son, Luciano, is incredibly friendly and adds to the family feel. We discovered the joint nearly 4 years ago and eat here or order pickup nearly every single week. With a wide variety of pastas and the best pizza west of north Jersey, there‚Äôs something for everyone. Even our picky son loves everything here. When a baby, Pietro, himself, used to come out and personally cut up meatballs for our son. Very family friendly. The last restaurant of a dying breed, we hope they stick around forever! Do yourself a favor, and help keep small local businesses around during three tough times...check them out!< /Text><Name>Rali Schwartz< /Name>< response>

<Text>I love all kinds of pizza and the places that make them. Like the inexpensive Little Caesar's to the filling kinds like New York Giant. However, if I want a truly authentic pizza made by a warm hearted passionate Italian, then I will always go to Pietro's. Seriously, with your first bite of pizza, you notice perfection in the ingredients and this amazing balance of each layer. Like how he can have this thin layer of sauce, not too wet or dry, and have it be the perfect amount. Also, where I could carb out on other pizzas, two slices of Pietro's pizza fills me up for less money than I would pay at another place. I think this is because Pietro's pizza crust is more authentic and not just bread.<//Text>< rate>

I really like this place, obviously. Let me start by saying from the outside it is fairly understated, tucked into the corner of a strip mall in La Mesa. Walk in and you are warmly-welcomed, often times by the Maestro himself. The d√©cor is fairly standard Italian-themed restaurant, but the atmosphere is jovial and welcoming. < Text>
Friday, May 17, 2019

Location:
1940 N Main St, Salinas, CA 93906

PARKING:
Plenty of free parking.

ADA:
ADA parking at front door.
Looks like nearly all tables are wheelchair accessible.

BATHROOMS:
Bathrooms are clean.
No foul odors.

FOOD:
Menu is quite complete.
This is a Viet Namese Restaurant.
Don't expect to find other Asian items on the menu.
The food looks and tastes like the food served to me in Viet Nam.

Portions are ample.
You'll not walk away hungry.
Unless you are a glutton.

Prices are reasonable.

This is a great place to lunch or enjoy a casual dinner with your Sweetheart.
Nothing formal here.
T-shirt, shorts and sandals are welcome here.

Staff is pleasant.
They understand and speak English well.
However, they've an Asian ear for language.
In my case, the waitress misunderstood white rice for fried rice.

I'll return, and recommend this restaurant to my beautiful Sleeping Beauty.< /Text>

<Review>I've been coming here for a couple of years now, and I noticed a lot of the reviews are a bit unfair. You come here for a traditional Thai massage, like you would actually get in Thailand. The masseuses are even all from Thailand. I've had my fair share of Thai massages in Thailand; from the decor, to the setup of the rooms, to the actual massages, it's a really authentic experience to what you'll get in Thailand.

Thai massage therapists are there to really work you over and beat you into submission. If you've got knots or any body soreness, they will ruthlessly attack it. Might be a little (or a lot) painful during, but you leave feeling loose. This includes using their feet and body weight to really loosen the muscles. And as with all traditional Thai massages, you lay on a cushion on the floor, rather than a table.

PSA - it's a cash-only establishment. They has free parking which is a great perk in LA these days!< /Review><time>1595823388403</time><Rate>4<//Rate><UserId.>102164257455415032236<//UserId.></record></dataset><record>
